.. _group___cmp_app_itf:

=========
CmpAppItf
=========

.. contents::
    :local:
    :depth: 1

Interface of CmpApp.

Detailed Description
--------------------

This is the interface of the IEC application manager. The manager is responsible for:

  - Handles and collects all IEC applications

  - Application specific online communication to the programming system (debugging, forcing, etc.)

  - Code and data handling (areas)

  - Handling of non volatile data (retain handling)

An IEC application is a set of objects which are needed for running a particular instance of the PLC program. Each application is specified by its unique name.

Applications can have relationships among each other. If one application e.g. A2 depends from another application A1, A1 is the parent and A2 the child. So A2 is derived from A1.

Each application has two different kind of states:

  - Application state: run, stop, exception, etc.

  - Operating state: storing boot application, do online-change, etc.

The application state is used to specify, if the application is operating normal or not. The operating state is used to specify, which job is executed in the moment on the application.

An IEC application consists of one or more tasks. The IEC tasks are not handled directly by the application manager. This is provided by the IEC task manager. See CmpIecTask for detailed information.

An application can have code and data. So the application manager needs for each application one or more memory areas in which the code and data will be administrated.

typedef struct tagappgetsegmentaddress_struct  appgetsegmentaddress_struct
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function returns the start address of an IEC segment. All segments resides within an area. This is used to get access for example to the beginning of the output process image segment (Q = AreaType.DA_OUTPUT).

**Parameters**

+---------+---------+------------------------+
| [in]    | pApp    | Pointer to Application |
+---------+---------+------------------------+
| [in]    | wType   | Area type              |
+---------+---------+------------------------+
| [in]    | pResult | Pointer to Result      |
+---------+---------+------------------------+

**Returns:**

Segment start address

+---------+---------+------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1ga07319c8fc1225782ffc6699b6ffd57ab:

APPLICATION* AppCreateApplication (char *pszAppName, char *pszAppParentName, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Creates an application specified by name

**Parameters**

+---------+------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszAppName       | Pointer to name of the application                                                                 |
+---------+------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszAppParentName | Pointer to name of the parent application (if a child application should be created). Can be NULL. |
+---------+------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult          | Pointer to error code                                                                              |
+---------+------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Pointer to the application description

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1gaeefe3e296c83e3ad66951597889573e1:

RTS_RESULT AppPrepareDownload (APPLICATION *pApp, int bOnlineChange, int bCreateBootproject)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Prepares a new download or online-change

**Parameters**

+---------+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pApp               | Pointer to the specified application description                     |
+---------+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | bOnlineChange      | 1=Online change, 0=Download                                          |
+---------+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | bCreateBootproject | 1=Create implicitly a boot application, 0=Create no boot application |
+---------+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1ga124ee30203d80b8f90ae157313076c84:

RTS_RESULT AppAppendCode (APPLICATION *pApp, RTS_UI8 *pbyCode, RTS_SIZE ulCodeLen, RTS_SIZE ulCodeOffset, int bLoadBootproject)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Append IEC code for each code fragment. NOTE: Actually only available for CmpAppEmbedded!

**Parameters**

+---------+------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pApp             | Pointer to the specified application description                                     |
+---------+------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pbyCode          | Pointer to code part                                                                 |
+---------+------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulCodeLen        | Code fragment length                                                                 |
+---------+------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulCodeOffset     | Code offset of the fragment, to write to                                             |
+---------+------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | bLoadBootproject | 1=Function is called at loading boot application, 0=Else (e.g. at download sequence) |
+---------+------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1ga218c57bd97ba470a169ced36beefaaa5:

RTS_RESULT AppHasAddress (APPLICATION *pApp, RTS_VOID_FCTPTR pAddress)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Function checks, if the address is a part of the specified application (resides in an area). This function will although check if the address is part of an parent application.

**Parameters**

+---------+----------+----------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pApp     | Application                                                    |
+---------+----------+----------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pAddress | Pointer to check. Can be a data pointer or a function pointer. |
+---------+----------+----------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

ERR_OK: pAddress is part of the specified application ERR_FAILED: pAddress is not a part of the specified application

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1ga70cdc252e451f68736a57e076a7f8efc:

RTS_RESULT AppHasAddress2 (APPLICATION *pApp, RTS_VOID_FCTPTR pAddress, RTS_BOOL bIncludeParents)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Function checks, if the address is a part of the specified application (resides in an area)

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pApp            | Application                                                                                            |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pAddress        | Pointer to check. Can be a data pointer or a function pointer.                                         |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | bIncludeParents | Flag to indicate if only the current application, or although the parent applications must be checked. |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

ERR_OK: pAddress is part of the specified application ERR_FAILED: pAddress is not a part of the specified application

| [in]    | ulTimeoutMs  | Timeout in milliseconds to wait for stop. RTS_TIMEOUT_DEFAULT can be used as the default value |
+---------+--------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulStopReason | Stop reason, See corresponding category                                                        |
+---------+--------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code

**Return values**

+---------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK        | Application could be stopped and is now in state AS_STOP      |
+---------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER | Invalid parameter                                             |
+---------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_TIMEOUT   | Application could not be stopped within the specified timeout |
+---------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_FAILED    | Application failed to stop                                    |
+---------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1ga328a89d02adfd171ea0be0c4c6c0cc89:

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1gaedfe141f230ca8ad832aac09e4e0a92d:

RTS_HANDLE AppConsistencyCheckBegin (APPLICATION *pApp, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Begin a consistency sequence. This can be used to check, if any task of an IEC application (or its father application) was active during this sequence. A typical usage is the task consistent data monitoring during this sequence.

**Parameters**

+---------+---------+----------------------------+
| [in]    | pApp    | Pointer to the application |
+---------+---------+----------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult | Pointer to error code      |
+---------+---------+----------------------------+

**Returns:**

Return a handle to the consistency object

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1gada89122fff08ca42a6566fa8403365ca:

RTS_RESULT AppConsistencyCheckEnd (RTS_HANDLE hConsistency)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

End a consistency sequence. This can be used to check, if any task of an IEC application (or its father application) was active during this consistency sequence. A typical usage is the task consistent data monitoring.

**Parameters**

+---------+--------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hConsistency | Handle to the consistency object that is returned by AppConsistencyBegin() |
+---------+--------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

ERR_OK: No task active during this consistency sequence, ERR_FAILED: Any task of this application was active during this sequence

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1gad4b08a6a4eaa396500f0a7ce5648c34e:

RTS_RESULT AppConsistencyCheckAll (void)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Check all applications for consistency, that are called with :ref:`AppConsistencyCheckBegin() <group___cmp_app_itf_1gaedfe141f230ca8ad832aac09e4e0a92d>`
**Returns:**

ERR_OK: No task active during this consistency sequence, ERR_FAILED: Any task of an application was active during this sequence

RTS_RESULT AppHasAccessRights (char *pszApplication, char *pszObject, RTS_UI32 ulRequestedRights, RTS_UI32 ulSessionId, BINTAGWRITER *pWriter)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Check the access rights to the specified object of the application

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------+

+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------+

+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1gac53f60507bc3c0837f4cdc787a01e580:

RTS_HANDLE AppGetFirstConfiguredBootproject (char *pszAppName, RTS_I32 nMaxAppName, RTS_BOOL bCheckFile, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Function to get the first configured boot application.

This pre-check may be called prior to the loading of any boot application when functions like AppGetFirstApp, AppGetNextApp, AppGetNumOfApplications are not yet initialized.

To get the next boot application, call AppGetNextConfiguredBootproject with the returned iteration handle.

IMPLEMENTATION NOTE: This function may be called prior to CH_INIT_TASKS but after CH_INIT

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pszAppName  | Pointer to the buffer for application name                        |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | nMaxAppName | Buffer size                                                       |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | bCheckFile  | If set the application file is checked and returned only if found |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult     | Pointer to error code                                             |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Return values**

+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK            | An application name is successfully found and returned. |
+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER     | Invalid parameter (pointer NULL or length 0)            |
+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_END_OF_OBJECT | No more entries found.                                  |
+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Iteration handle

.. _group___cmp_app_itf_1gad8855b4c95f7e244136f051acd56e2b5:

RTS_HANDLE AppGetNextConfiguredBootproject (RTS_HANDLE hPrev, char *pszAppName, RTS_I32 nMaxAppName, RTS_BOOL bCheckFile, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Function to get the next configured boot application.

This function is called at first with the iteration handle of AppGetFirstConfiguredBootproject. The next call requires the iteration handle of the previous call of AppGetNextConfiguredBootproject.

For more information see AppGetFirstConfiguredBootproject.

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hPrev       | Iteration handle from previous call of either AppGetFirstConfiguredBootproject or AppGetNextConfiguredBootproject |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pszAppName  | Pointer to the buffer for application name                                                                        |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | nMaxAppName | Buffer size                                                                                                       |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | bCheckFile  | If set the application file is checked and returned only if found                                                 |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult     | Pointer to error code                                                                                             |
+---------+-------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Return values**

+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK            | An application name is successfully found and returned. |
+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER     | Invalid parameter (pointer NULL or length 0)            |
+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_END_OF_OBJECT | No more entries found.                                  |
+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Iteration handle
